                                    2106 *FUNCTION                                                               21840021
                                    2107 * RESOLVES NAME QUALIFICATION.                                          21860021
                                    2108 * QUALIFIERS ENTER PHASE 3 IN REVERSE OF SOURCE ORDER, HIGHEST LEVE     21880021
                                    2109 * QUALIFIER FIRST, QUALIFIED NAME LAST.                                 21900021
                                    2110 * QUALIF CHECKS TO SEE IF THE HIGHEST LEVEL QUALIFIER IS UNIQUE,        21920021
                                    2111 * IF NOT A WARNING MESSAGE IS WRITTEN, THE ELEMENT IS DISCARDED         21940021
                                    2112 * AND PROCESSING CONTINUES ON THE REST OF THE STRING. IF THE            21960021
                                    2113 * HIGHEST LEVEL QUALIFIER IS UNIQUE, QUALIF CHECKS TO SEE               21980021
                                    2114 * THAT SUBSEQUENT QUALIFIERS AND THE QUALIFIED NAME ARE ON PROGRES-     22000021
                                    2115 * SIVELY LOWER LEVELS IN THE SAME HIERARCHY, AND THAT THE QUALIFIED     22020021
                                    2116 * NAME IS UNIQUELY IDENTIFIED BY ITS QUALIFIERS.  EXITS VIA SEARCH.     22040021
                                    2117 *                                                                       22060021
